# Investigation: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/envoy--25f893b4 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/envoy--25f893b4 (mirror of envoyproxy/envoy)
**Task Type:** Deep Causal Chain (investigation only — no code fixes)

## Scenario

An Envoy proxy operator reports that response headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` in route configuration are being **duplicated** in certain responses. Specifically, when the router filter generates a local reply (e.g., upstream timeout, connection failure, or request too large), custom response headers like `x-request-id-echo` appear twice in the HTTP response.

The issue is intermittent — it only affects responses where the router itself generates the reply (local replies) rather than forwarding an upstream response. Normal proxied responses have headers added exactly once.

Access log snippet showing the problem (using `%RESPONSE_CODE_DETAILS%` formatter):

```
[2025-08-15T10:23:45.001Z] "GET /api/v1/data HTTP/1.1" 504 UT
response_code_details=upstream_response_timeout
x-custom-trace: abc123
x-custom-trace: abc123
```

The header `x-custom-trace` appears twice. The route config has:

```yaml
response_headers_to_add:
  - header:
      key: "x-custom-trace"
      value: "%REQ(x-request-id)%"
    append_action: OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD
```

Despite using `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, the header is duplicated on local replies but not on proxied upstream responses.

## Your Task

Investigate the root cause of this duplicate header behavior and produce a report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`.

Your report MUST cover:

1. **How the router filter processes response headers** — specifically the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call chain and the `modify_headers_` callback
2. **How local replies are generated** — the `sendLocalReply` code path in the router and how it differs from the upstream response path
3. **The specific mechanism causing double processing** — which PR/change moved `finalizeResponseHeaders()` into the `modify_headers_` callback, and why this causes double invocation for local replies
4. **The interaction between `sendLocalReply` and `modify_headers_`** — how `sendLocalReply` calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` directly, AND the `modify_headers_` callback also calls it, resulting in headers being added twice
5. **The role of the `append_action` / `append` proto fields** — how `HeaderValueOption` config is parsed in `header_parser.cc`, including the deprecated `append` BoolValue field vs the newer `append_action` enum, and how proto default values affect behavior
6. **The filter manager's encode path** — how `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` iterates through filters in reverse order and how the header mutation filter interacts with route-level header additions
7. **Which files and functions form the full causal chain** from symptom (duplicate headers in access log) to root cause (double `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call)

## Output Requirements

Write your investigation report to `/logs/agent/investigation.md` with these sections:

```
# Investigation Report

## Summary
<1-2 sentence finding>

## Root Cause
<Specific file, function, and mechanism>

## Evidence
<Code references with file paths and line numbers>

## Affected Components
<List of packages/modules impacted>

## Causal Chain
<Ordered list: symptom → intermediate hops → root cause>

## Recommendation
<Fix strategy and diagnostic steps>
```

## Constraints

- Do NOT write any code fixes
- Do NOT modify any source files
- Your job is investigation and analysis only
- The causal chain spans at least 4 packages: `source/common/router/`, `source/common/http/`, `source/extensions/filters/http/header_mutation/`, and `api/envoy/config/core/v3/`

Perfect! I've completed the investigation and produced a detailed report at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`. 

## Summary

The investigation has identified the root cause of duplicate response headers in Envoy's router filter for local replies:

**Key Finding**: A double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` occurs when:
1. The filter manager's wrapping lambda (added in v1.35.0) calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` to apply `response_headers_to_add` to local replies
2. The router's direct response path simultaneously calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` within its own lambda

**Evidence Chain**:
- Router filter (`router.cc:501`) explicitly calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its lambda passed to `sendLocalReply()`
- Filter manager (`filter_manager.cc:1074`) wraps this with another call to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` before executing the router's lambda
- Header parser (`header_parser.cc:184-185`) appends headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` mode, causing duplicates when called twice
- The issue is enabled by the v1.35.0 feature that extended `response_headers_to_add` support to local replies

The report includes detailed code references, affected components across 4 packages, a complete causal chain from symptom to root cause, and diagnostic recommendations for implementing a fix.

If this assumption changes, the number of inlined capacity should be increased.\n160:   // header_formatter_speed_test.cc provides micro-benchmark for evaluating speed of adding and\n161:   // replacing headers and should be used when modifying the code below to access the performance\n162:   // impact of code changes.\n163:   absl::InlinedVector<std::pair<const Http::LowerCaseString&, const std::string>, 4> headers_to_add,\n164:       headers_to_overwrite;\n165:   // value_buffer is used only when stream_info is a valid pointer and stores header value\n166:   // created by a formatter. The\n168:   // actual value of the header is accessed via 'value' variable which is initialized differently\n169:   // depending whether stream_info and valid or nullptr. Based on performance tests implemented in\n170:   // header_formatter_speed_test.cc this approach strikes the best balance between performance and\n171:   // readability.\n172:   std::string value_buffer;\n173:   for (const auto& [key, entry] : headers_to_add_) {\n174:     absl::string_view value;\n175:     if (stream_info != nullptr) {\n176:       value_buffer = headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);\n186:         break;\n187:       case HeaderValueOption::ADD_IF_ABSENT:\n188:         if (auto header_entry = headers.get(key); header_entry.empty()) {\n189:           headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);\n190:         }\n191:         break;\n192:       case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS:\n193:         if (headers.get(key).empty()) {\n194:           break;\n195:         }\n196:         FALLTHRU;\n197:       case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n198:         headers_to_overwrite.emplace_back(key, value);\n199: headers.setReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);\n207:   }\n208: \n209:   // Now add headers which should be added.\n210:   for (const auto& header : headers_to_add) {\n211:     headers.addReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);\n212:   }\n213: }\n214: \n215: Http::HeaderTransforms HeaderParser::getHeaderTransforms(const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info,\n216: 42. Write @ -
Input
{
  "content": "# Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline\n\n## Summary\n\nResponse headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` are being duplicated in certain local replies generated by the router filter. The root cause is a double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` \u2014 once by the filter manager's wrapping lambda (added in v1.35.0 to support response headers in local replies) and once by the router filter's own lambda for direct response entries.\n\n## Root Cause\n\n**Location**: Interaction between `source/common/router/router.cc` and `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n**Mechanism**:\n1. The router filter's direct response path (`router.cc:486-503`) passes a lambda to `sendLocalReply()` that explicitly calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 501)\n2. The filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` method (`filter_manager.cc:1109-1130`) wraps this lambda in a new lambda that:\n   - First calls `streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (lines 1073-1074)\n   - Then calls the router's passed-in lambda (line 1077), which internally calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` again\n3. For certain routing configurations, both calls execute successfully, causing headers from `response_headers_to_add` to be added twice\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Router Filter - Direct Response Path\n**File**: `source/common/router/router.cc:486-503`\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),\n    [this, direct_response, &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {\n      // ...location header logic...\n      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL\n    },\n    absl::nullopt, StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().DirectResponse);\n```\n\n### Filter Manager - sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain Wrapper\n**File**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1109-1130` and `1070-1094`\n```cpp\nUtility::sendLocalReply(\n    state_.destroyed_,\n    Utility::EncodeFunctions{\n        [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n          if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n            streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // SECOND CALL\n          }\n          if (modify_headers) {\n            modify_headers(headers);  // This also calls finalizeResponseHeaders for direct response case\n          }\n        },\n        // ... other encode functions ...\n    },\n    Utility::LocalReplyData{...});\n```\n\n### Header Parser - How Headers Are Added\n**File**: `source/common/router/header_parser.cc:139-213`\n\nThe `evaluateHeaders()` method in `HeaderParser` processes each configured header based on its `append_action`:\n- `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Appends to existing header or adds if absent\n- `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`: Overwrites or adds if absent\n- `ADD_IF_ABSENT`: Only adds if header doesn't exist\n\nWhen `finalizeResponseHeaders()` calls `evaluateHeaders()`, it iterates through all configured headers and applies them. If called twice with the same headers map, headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` will be appended twice.\n\n### Route Entry Implementation\n**File**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h:628-630`\n\n`RouteEntryImplBase` inherits from both `RouteEntryAndRoute` and `DirectResponseEntry`, making it simultaneously a route entry and direct response entry. This dual inheritance is central to the issue.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **source/common/router/router.cc**\n   - `Filter::decodeHeaders()` \u2014 Initializes route and determines if direct response exists\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` \u2014 Sends local replies for timeout/connection failures (line 1403)\n   - Direct response handling path (lines 486-503)\n\n2. **source/common/http/filter_manager.cc**\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` \u2014 Entry point for local reply handling (line 982)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` \u2014 Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1055)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` \u2014 Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1109)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendDirectLocalReply()` \u2014 Wraps modify_headers callback (line 1147)\n\n3. **source/common/router/config_impl.cc**\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders()` \u2014 Evaluates header parsers (line 942)\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::directResponseEntry()` \u2014 Returns `this` for direct responses (line 1287)\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::routeEntry()` \u2014 Returns `nullptr` for direct responses (line 1297)\n\n4. **source/common/router/header_parser.cc**\n   - `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` \u2014 Applies headers based on append_action (line 139)\n   - `HeadersToAddEntry` \u2014 Parses deprecated `append` field vs new `append_action` enum (line 53)\n\n5. **api/envoy/config/core/v3/**\n   - `HeaderValueOption` proto \u2014 Contains both deprecated `append: BoolValue` and new `append_action: enum`\n   - Proto default for `append_action` is `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Access logs show duplicate response headers in local replies\n   - Example: `x-custom-trace: abc123` appears twice despite `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` config\n\n2. **Path to Root Cause**:\n   - Local reply is generated by router (timeout/error condition)\n   - Router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply(code, body, modify_headers_lambda, ...)`\n   - For direct response paths, the lambda includes `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - `sendLocalReply()` delegates to filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n   - Filter manager creates a wrapping lambda that adds another `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call\n   - Both calls execute, evaluating header parsers twice\n   - Headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` (default) get appended twice\n\n3. **Enabling Change**: v1.35.0 added response header support for local replies\n   - Added `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call to filter manager's wrapping lambda (line 1074, 1125, 1158)\n   - This was intended to apply `response_headers_to_add` from route config to local replies\n   - Did not account for cases where the route's lambda already calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n## Interaction Between Components\n\n1. **Router Filter's Role**:\n   - Determines if route has direct response entry\n   - If yes, passes lambda to `sendLocalReply()` that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - If no (normal route), passes `modify_headers_` lambda that only adds attempt count header\n\n2. **Filter Manager's Wrapping**:\n   - Receives the router's lambda as `modify_headers` parameter\n   - Creates a NEW lambda that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` first (if route entry exists)\n   - Then calls the passed-in lambda\n   - This wrapping happens for both `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` and `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n\n3. **Header Parser Behavior**:\n   - Each call to `evaluateHeaders()` iterates through all configured headers\n   - Headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` are appended via `headers.addReferenceKey()`\n   - When called twice on same headers map, appends happen twice\n   - # Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline

## Summary

Response headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` are being duplicated in certain local replies generated by the router filter. The root cause is a double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` — once by the filter manager's wrapping lambda (added in v1.35.0 to support response headers in local replies) and once by the router filter's own lambda for direct response entries.

## Root Cause

**Location**: Interaction between `source/common/router/router.cc` and `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`

**Mechanism**:
1. The router filter's direct response path (`router.cc:486-503`) passes a lambda to `sendLocalReply()` that explicitly calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 501)
2. The filter manager's `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` method (`filter_manager.cc:1109-1130`) wraps this lambda in a new lambda that:
   - First calls `streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (lines 1073-1074)
   - Then calls the router's passed-in lambda (line 1077), which internally calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` again
3. For certain routing configurations, both calls execute successfully, causing headers from `response_headers_to_add` to be added twice

## Evidence

### Router Filter - Direct Response Path
**File**: `source/common/router/router.cc:486-503`
```cpp
callbacks_->sendLocalReply(
    direct_response->responseCode(), direct_response->responseBody(),
    [this, direct_response, &request_headers = headers](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& response_headers) -> void {
      // ...location header logic...
      direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders(response_headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL
    },
    absl::nullopt, StreamInfo::ResponseC
... (truncated)
